While teams like Lahore will aim to regain their former glory, the other teams will want to win this title.</p><div id="ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-141" data-inserter-version="2" data-placement-location="incontent_13"></div><script data-ezoic="1" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" type="edc5b46a445cf84e68f5e800-text/javascript">ezstandalone.cmd.push(function () { ezstandalone.showAds(141); });</script><p>What will happen?
